CNN for Image Classification (Animals vs Vehicles)\n#####################################\n\ndef prepare_cifar10_animals_vehicles():\n    \"\"\"\n    Load CIFAR-10 and select animals (cat, dog, horse, deer, frog, bird) and vehicles (automobile, truck, airplane, ship).\n    Returns X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test where y=0 for animal, y=1 for vehicle.\n    \"\"\"\n    print(\"\\n=== CNN: Image Classification (Animals vs Vehicles) ===\")\n    (X_train, y_train), (X_test, y_test) = tf.keras.datasets.cifar10.load_data()\n    y_train = y_train.flatten()\n    y_test = y_test.flatten()\n    # CIFAR-10 classes\n    animal_classes = [2, 3, 4, 5, 6, 7]  # bird, cat, deer, dog, frog, horse\n    vehicle_classes = [0, 1, 8, 9]        # airplane, automobile, ship, truck\n    \n    def filter_data(X, y):\n        idx_animal = np.isin(y, animal_classes)\n        idx_vehicle = np.isin(y, vehicle_classes)\n        X_animal = X[idx_animal]\n        y_animal = np.zeros(X_animal.shape[0], dtype=int)\n        X_vehicle = X[idx_vehicle]\n        y_vehicle = np.ones(X_vehicle.shape[0], dtype=int)\n        X_filtered = np.concatenate([X_animal, X_vehicle], axis=0)\n        y_filtered = np.concatenate([y_animal, y_vehicle], axis=0)\n        return X_filtered, y_filtered\n    \n    X_train_f, y_train_f = filter_data(X_train, y_train)\n    X_test_f, y_test_f = filter_data(X_test, y_test)\n    \n    # Normalize images\n    X_train_f = X_train_f.astype('float32') / 255.0\n    X_test_f = X_test_f.astype('float32') / 255.0\n    \n    # Shuffle\n    idx = np.arange(X_train_f.shape[0])\n    np.random.shuffle(idx)\n    X_train_f, y_train_f = X_train_f[idx], y_train_f[idx]\n    \n    idx = np.arange(X_test_f.shape[0])\n    np.random.shuffle(idx)\n    X_test_f, y_test_f = X_test_f[idx], y_test_f[idx]\n    \n    return X_train_f, X_test_f, y_train_f, y_test_f\n\ndef build_transfer_cnn(input_shape):\n    \"\"\"\n    Build a CNN using transfer learning from MobileNetV2.\n    \"\"\"\n    base_model = applications.MobileNetV2(\n        input_shape=input_shape, include_top=False, weights='imagenet', pooling='avg'\n    )\n    base_model.trainable = False  # Freeze base\n    model = models.Sequential([\n        base_model,\n        layers.Dense(128, activation='relu'),\n        layers.Dropout(0.3),\n        layers.Dense(1, activation='sigmoid')\n    ])\n    model.compile(\n        optimizer='adam',\n        loss='binary_crossentropy',\n        metrics=['accuracy']\n    )\n    return model\n\ndef evaluate_cnn_classification(y_true, y_pred, y_prob):\n    \"\"\"\n    Print evaluation metrics for CNN binary classification.\n    \"\"\"\n    print(\"Accuracy:  {:.4f}\".format(accuracy_score(y_true, y_pred)))\n    print(\"Precision: {:.4f}\".format(precision_score(y_true, y_pred)))\n    print(\"Recall:    {:.4f}\".format(recall_score(y_true, y_pred)))\n    print(\"F1 Score:  {:.4f}\".format(f1_score(y_true, y_pred)))\n    print(\"\\nClassification Report:\\n\", classification_report(y_true, y_pred, target_names=['Animal','Vehicle']))\n    cm = confusion_matrix(y_true, y_pred)\n    plt.figure(figsize=(4, 4))\n    plt.imshow(cm, cmap='Blues')\n    plt.title(\"Confusion Matrix (CNN)\")\n    plt.xlabel(\"Predicted\")\n    plt.ylabel(\"Actual\")\n    plt.colorbar()\n    plt.xticks([0,1], ['Animal','Vehicle'])\n    plt.yticks([0,1], ['Animal','Vehicle'])\n    for i in range(2):\n        for j in range(2):\n            plt.text(j, i, cm[i, j], ha='center', va='center', color='red')\n    plt.tight_layout()\n    plt.show()\n\ndef cnn_image_classification_pipeline():\n    \"\"\"\n    Full pipeline for image classification using transfer learning CNN.\n    \"\"\"\n    X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = prepare_cifar10_animals_vehicles()\n    # MobileNetV2 expects at least 32x32x3, so we can use CIFAR-10's 32x32x3 directly\n    input_shape = (32, 32, 3)\n    model = build_transfer_cnn(input_shape)\n    # Use a small subset for quick training\n    n_train = 5000\n    n_test = 1000\n    history = model.fit(\n        X_train[:n_train], y_train[:n_train],\n        epochs=5, batch_size=32,\n        validation_split=0.1, verbose=1\n    )\n    y_prob = model.predict(X_test[:n_test]).flatten()\n    y_pred = (y_prob > 0.5).astype(int)\n    evaluate_cnn_classification(y_test[:n_test], y_pred, y_prob)\n\n#####################################\n# Main\n#####################################\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    dnn_network_traffic_pipeline()\n    cnn_image_classification_pipeline()",
                        "\"\"\"\nMachine Learning Pipelines:\n1. DNN for Network Traffic Classification (Malicious/Safe)\n2. CNN for Image Classification (Animals vs Vehicles) with Transfer Learning\n\nAuthor: [Your Name]\nDate: 2024-06-XX\n\nQuick Start Guide:\n------------------\n1. Install requirements:\n    pip install numpy pandas scikit-learn tensorflow matplotlib\n\n2. Run the script:\n    python ml_pipelines.py\n\nThe script will:\n- Train and evaluate a DNN on synthetic network traffic data.\n- Train and evaluate a CNN (with transfer learning) on a subset of CIFAR-10 (animals vs vehicles).\n- Print evaluation metrics and plot confusion matrices.\n\nDocumentation:\n--------------\n- DNN Pipeline:\n    - Generates synthetic network traffic data with categorical and numerical features.\n    - Preprocesses features (encoding, scaling).\n    - Trains a DNN for binary classification (malicious/safe).\n    - Evaluates using accuracy, precision, recall, F1, confusion matrix.\n\n- CNN Pipeline:\n    - Loads CIFAR-10 and selects animal/vehicle classes.\n    - Normalizes and shuffles data.\n    - Uses MobileNetV2 for transfer learning.\n    - Trains a CNN for binary classification (animal/vehicle).\n    - Evaluates using accuracy, precision, recall, F1, confusion matrix.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport os\nimport numpy as np\nimport pandas as pd\nimport matplotlib.pyplot as plt\nfrom sklearn.model_selection import train_test_split\nfrom sklearn.metrics import (\n    accuracy_score, precision_score, recall_score, f1_score, confusion_matrix, classification_report\n)\nfrom sklearn.preprocessing import StandardScaler, LabelEncoder\nimport tensorflow as tf\nfrom tensorflow.keras import layers, models, applications\n\n# Set random seeds for reproducibility\nnp.random.seed(42)\ntf.random.set_seed(42)\n\n#####################################\n# 1. DNN for Network Traffic Classification\n#####################################\n\ndef generate_synthetic_network_data(n_samples=5000):\n    \"\"\"\n    Generate synthetic network traffic data.\n    Features: duration, protocol_type, service, src_bytes, dst_bytes, flag, land, wrong_fragment, urgent\n    Label: 0 (safe), 1 (malicious)\n    \"\"\"\n    protocols = ['tcp', 'udp', 'icmp']\n    services = ['http', 'ftp', 'smtp', 'dns', 'ssh']\n    flags = ['SF', 'S0', 'REJ', 'RSTR']\n    \n    data = {\n        'duration': np.random.exponential(scale=2, size=n_samples),\n        'protocol_type': np.random.choice(protocols, n_samples),\n        'service': np.random.choice(services, n_samples),\n        'src_bytes': np.random.randint(0, 10000, n_samples),\n        'dst_bytes': np.random.randint(0, 10000, n_samples),\n        'flag': np.random.choice(flags, n_samples),\n        'land': np.random.binomial(1, 0.05, n_samples),\n        'wrong_fragment': np.random.randint(0, 3, n_samples),\n        'urgent': np.random.randint(0, 2, n_samples),\n    }\n    df = pd.DataFrame(data)\n    \n    # Simple logic: traffic with high src_bytes, wrong_fragment, or urgent is more likely malicious\n    malicious_prob = (\n        0.2 * (df['src_bytes'] > 5000).astype(float) +\n        0.2 * (df['wrong_fragment'] > 0).astype(float) +\n        0.2 * (df['urgent'] > 0).astype(float) +\n        0.1 * (df['protocol_type'] == 'icmp').astype(float) +\n        0.1 * (df['flag'] == 'REJ').astype(float)\n    )\n    labels = np.random.binomial(1, malicious_prob.clip(0, 0.95))\n    df['label'] = labels\n    return df\n\ndef preprocess_network_data(df):\n    \"\"\"\n    Encode categorical features and scale numerical features.\n    Returns:\n        X_scaled: numpy array of features\n        y: numpy array of labels\n    \"\"\"\n    X = df.drop('label', axis=1)\n    y = df['label'].values\n    \n    # Encode categorical features\n    for col in ['protocol_type', 'service', 'flag']:\n        le = LabelEncoder()\n        X[col] = le.fit_transform(X[col])\n    \n    # Scale features\n    scaler = StandardScaler()\n    X_scaled = scaler.fit_transform(X)\n    return X_scaled, y\n\ndef build_dnn_model(input_dim):\n    \"\"\"\n    Build a simple DNN model for binary classification.\n    Args:\n        input_dim: int, number of input features\n    Returns:\n        model: compiled Keras model\n    \"\"\"\n    model = models.Sequential([\n        layers.Input(shape=(input_dim,)),\n        layers.Dense(32, activation='relu'),\n        layers.Dense(16, activation='relu'),\n        layers.Dense(1, activation='sigmoid')\n    ])\n    model.compile(\n        optimizer='adam',\n        loss='binary_crossentropy',\n        metrics=['accuracy']\n    )\n    return model\n\ndef evaluate_binary_classification(y_true, y_pred, y_prob):\n    \"\"\"\n    Print evaluation metrics for binary classification.\n    Args:\n        y_true: true labels\n        y_pred: predicted labels\n        y_prob: predicted probabilities\n    \"\"\"\n    print(\"Accuracy:  {:.4f}\".format(accuracy_score(y_true, y_pred)))\n    print(\"Precision: {:.4f}\".format(precision_score(y_true, y_pred)))\n    print(\"Recall:    {:.4f}\".format(recall_score(y_true, y_pred)))\n    print(\"F1 Score:  {:.4f}\".format(f1_score(y_true, y_pred)))\n    print(\"\\nClassification Report:\\n\", classification_report(y_true, y_pred, target_names=['Safe','Malicious']))\n    cm = confusion_matrix(y_true, y_pred)\n    plt.figure(figsize=(4, 4))\n    plt.imshow(cm, cmap='Blues')\n    plt.title(\"Confusion Matrix\")\n    plt.xlabel(\"Predicted\")\n    plt.ylabel(\"Actual\")\n    plt.colorbar()\n    plt.xticks([0,1], ['Safe','Malicious'])\n    plt.yticks([0,1], dnn_network_traffic_pipeline():\n    \"\"\"\n    Complete pipeline for DNN-based network traffic classification.\n    \"\"\"\n    print(\"\\n=== DNN: Network Traffic Classification ===\")\n    df = generate_synthetic_network_data()\n    X, y = preprocess_network_data(df)\n    X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(\n        X, y, test_size=0.2, stratify=y, random_state=42\n    )\n    model = build_dnn_model(X.shape[1])\n    history = model.fit(\n        X_train, y_train, epochs=15, batch_size=32,\n        validation_split=0.1, verbose=0\n    )\n    y_prob = model.predict(X_test).flatten()\n    y_pred = (y_prob > 0.5).astype(int)\n    evaluate_binary_classification(y_test, y_pred, y_prob)\n\n#####################################\n# 2. CNN for Image Classification (Animals vs Vehicles)\n#####################################\n\ndef prepare_cifar10_animals_vehicles():\n    \"\"\"\n    Load CIFAR-10 and select animals (cat, dog, horse, deer, frog, bird) and vehicles (automobile, truck, airplane, ship).\n    Returns X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test where y=0 for animal, y=1 for vehicle.\n    \"\"\"\n    print(\"\\n=== CNN: Image Classification (Animals vs Vehicles) ===\")\n    (X_train, y_train), (X_test, y_test) = tf.keras.datasets.cifar10.load_data()\n    y_train = y_train.flatten()\n    y_test = y_test.flatten()\n    # CIFAR-10 classes\n    animal_classes = [2, 3, 4, 5, 6, 7]  # bird, cat, deer, dog, frog, horse\n    vehicle_classes = [0, 1, 8, 9]        # airplane, automobile, ship, truck\n    \n    def filter_data(X, y):\n        idx_animal = np.isin(y, animal_classes)\n        idx_vehicle = np.isin(y, vehicle_classes)\n        X_animal = X[idx_animal]\n        y_animal = np.zeros(X_animal.shape[0], dtype=int)\n        X_vehicle = X[idx_vehicle]\n        y_vehicle = np.ones(X_vehicle.shape[0], dtype=int)\n        X_filtered = np.concatenate([X_animal, X_vehicle], axis=0)\n        y_filtered = np.concatenate([y_animal, y_vehicle], axis=0)\n        return X_filtered, y_filtered\n    \n    X_train_f, y_train_f = filter_data(X_train, y_train)\n    X_test_f, y_test_f = filter_data(X_test, y_test)\n    \n    # Freeze base\n    model = models.Sequential([\n        base_model,\n        layers.Dense(128, activation='relu'),\n        layers.Dropout(0.3),\n        layers.Dense(1, activation='sigmoid')\n    ])\n    model.compile(\n        optimizer='adam',\n        loss='binary_crossentropy',\n        metrics=['accuracy']\n    )\n    return model\n\ndef evaluate_cnn_classification(y_true, y_pred, y_prob):\n    \"\"\"\n    Print evaluation metrics for CNN binary classification.\n    Args:\n        y_true: true labels\n        y_pred: predicted labels\n        y_prob: predicted probabilities\n    \"\"\"\n    print(\"Accuracy:  {:.4f}\".format(accuracy_score(y_true, y_pred)))\n    print(\"Precision: {:.4f}\".format(precision_score(y_true, y_pred)))\n    print(\"Recall:    {:.4f}\".format(recall_score(y_true, y_pred)))\n    print(\"F1 Score:  {:.4f}\".format(f1_score(y_true, y_pred)))\n    print(\"\\nClassification Report:\\n\", classification_report(y_true, y_pred, target_names=['Animal','Vehicle']))\n    cm = confusion_matrix(y_true, y_pred)\n    plt.figure(figsize=(4, 4))\n    plt.imshow(cm, cmap='Blues')\n    plt.title(\"Confusion Matrix\")\n    plt.xlabel(\"Predicted\")\n    plt.ylabel(\"Actual\")\n    plt.colorbar()\n    plt.xticks([0,1], ['Animal','Vehicle'])\n    plt.yticks([0,1], ['Animal','Vehicle'])\n    for i in range(2):\n        for j in range(2):\n            plt.text(j, i, cm[i, j], ha='center', va='center', color='red')\n    plt.tight_layout()\n    plt.show()\n\ndef cnn_image_classification_pipeline():\n    \"\"\"\n    Complete pipeline for CNN-based animal/vehicle image classification using transfer learning.\n    \"\"\"\n    X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = prepare_cifar10_animals_vehicles()\n    # MobileNetV2 expects at least 32x32x3, so we can use CIFAR-10's 32x32x3 directly\n    input_shape = (32, 32, 3)\n    model = build_transfer_cnn(input_shape)\n    # Use a small subset for quick training\n    n_train = 5000\n    n_test = 1000\n    history = model.fit(\n        X_train[:n_train], y_train[:n_train],\n        epochs=5, batch_size=32,\n        validation_split=0.1, verbose=1\n    )\n    y_prob = model.predict(X_test[:n_test]).flatten()\n    y_pred = (y_prob > 0.5).astype(int)\n    evaluate_cnn_classification(y_test[:n_test], y_pred, y_prob)\n\n#####################################\n# Main\n#####################################\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    dnn_network_traffic_pipeline()\n    cnn_image_classification_pipeline()"

                        "import unittest\nimport numpy as np\nimport pandas as pd\nimport tensorflow as tf\nfrom tensorflow.keras import models\nimport types\nimport sys\n\n# Import the functions from generate_synthetic_network_data(n_samples=5000):\n    protocols = ['tcp', 'udp', 'icmp']\n    services = ['http', 'ftp', 'smtp', 'dns', 'ssh']\n    flags = ['SF', 'S0', 'REJ', 'RSTR']\n    \n    data = {\n        'duration': np.random.exponential(scale=2, size=n_samples),\n        'protocol_type': np.random.choice(protocols, n_samples),\n        'service': np.random.choice(services, n_samples),\n        'src_bytes': np.random.randint(0, 10000, n_samples),\n        'dst_bytes': np.random.randint(0, 10000, n_samples),\n        'flag': np.random.choice(flags, n_samples),\n        'land': np.random.binomial(1, 0.05, n_samples),\n        'wrong_fragment': np.random.randint(0, 3, n_samples),\n        'urgent': np.random.randint(0, 2, n_samples),\n    }\n    df = pd.DataFrame(data)\n    malicious_prob = (\n        0.2 * (df['src_bytes'] > 5000).astype(float) +\n        0.2 * (df['wrong_fragment'] > 0).astype(float) +\n        0.2 * (df['urgent'] > 0).astype(float) +\n        0.1 * (df['protocol_type'] == 'icmp').astype(float) +\n        0.1 * (df['flag'] == 'REJ').astype(float)\n    )\n    labels = np.random.binomial(1, malicious_prob.clip(0, 0.95))\n    df['label'] = labels\n    return df\n\ndef preprocess_network_data(df):\n    from sklearn.preprocessing import StandardScaler, LabelEncoder\n    X = df.drop('label', axis=1)\n    y = df['label'].values\n    for col in ['protocol_type', 'service', 'flag']:\n        le = LabelEncoder()\n        X[col] = le.fit_transform(X[col])\n    scaler = StandardScaler()\n    X_scaled = scaler.fit_transform(X)\n    return X_scaled, y\n\ndef build_dnn_model(input_dim):\n    from tensorflow.keras import layers, models\n    model = models.Sequential([\n        layers.Input(shape=(input_dim,)),\n        layers.Dense(32, activation='relu'),\n        layers.Dense(16, activation='relu'),\n        layers.Dense(1, activation='sigmoid')\n    ])\n    model.compile(\n        optimizer='adam',\n        loss='binary_crossentropy',\n        metrics=['accuracy']\n    )\n    return model\n\ndef prepare_cifar10_animals_vehicles():\n    (X_train, y_train), (X_test, y_test) = tf.keras.datasets.cifar10.load_data()\n    y_train = y_train.flatten()\n    y_test = y_test.flatten()\n    animal_classes = [2, 3, 4, 5, 6, 7]\n    vehicle_classes = [0, 1, 8, 9]\n    def filter_data(X, y):\n        idx_animal = np.isin(y, animal_classes)\n        idx_vehicle = np.isin(y, vehicle_classes)\n        X_animal = X[idx_animal]\n        y_animal = np.zeros(X_animal.shape[0], dtype=int)\n        X_vehicle = X[idx_vehicle]\n        y_vehicle = np.ones(X_vehicle.shape[0], dtype=int)\n        X_filtered = np.concatenate([X_animal, X_vehicle], axis=0)\n        y_filtered = np.concatenate([y_animal, y_vehicle], axis=0)\n        return X_filtered, y_filtered\n    X_train_f, y_train_f = filter_data(X_train, y_train)\n    X_test_f, y_test_f = filter_data(X_test, y_test)\n    X_train_f = X_train_f.astype('float32') / 255.0\n    X_test_f = X_test_f.astype('float32') / 255.0\n    idx = np.arange(X_train_f.shape[0])\n    np.random.shuffle(idx)\n    X_train_f, y_train_f = X_train_f[idx], y_train_f[idx]\n    idx = np.arange(X_test_f.shape[0])\n    np.random.shuffle(idx)\n    X_test_f, y_test_f = X_test_f[idx], y_test_f[idx]\n    return X_train_f, X_test_f, y_train_f, y_test_f\n\ndef build_transfer_cnn(input_shape):\n    from tensorflow.keras import layers, models, applications\n    base_model = applications.MobileNetV2(\n        input_shape=input_shape, include_top=False, weights=None, pooling='avg'\n    )\n    base_model.trainable = False\n    model = models.Sequential([\n        base_model,\n        layers.Dense(128, activation='relu'),\n        layers.Dropout(0.3),\n        layers.Dense(1, activation='sigmoid')\n    ])\n    model.compile(\n        optimizer='adam',\n        loss='binary_crossentropy',\n        metrics=['accuracy']\n    )\n    return model\n\n# --- End: Copied code from original script ---\n\nclass TestMLPipelines(unittest.TestCase):\n\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Set seeds for reproducibility in tests\n        np.random.seed(123)\n        tf.random.set_seed(123)\n\n    # --- DNN for Network Traffic Classification ---\n\n    def test_generate_synthetic_network_data_shape_and_columns(self):\n        df =               'flag', 'land', 'wrong_fragment', 'urgent', 'label'}\n        self.assertTrue(expected_columns.issubset(set(df.columns)))\n\n    def                         "import unittest\nimport numpy as np\nimport pandas as pd\nimport types\nimport sys\n\n# Import the code to test\n# Since the code is not in a module, we need to copy the -- BEGIN: Copied functions from the code to test --\n\ndef generate_synthetic_network_data(n_samples=5000):\n    protocols = ['tcp', 'udp', 'icmp']\n    services = ['http', 'ftp', 'smtp', 'dns', 'ssh']\n    flags = ['SF', 'S0', 'REJ', 'RSTR']\n    \n    data = {\n        'duration': np.random.exponential(scale=2, size=n_samples),\n        'protocol_type': np.random.choice(protocols, n_samples),\n        'service': np.random.choice(services, n_samples),\n        'src_bytes': np.random.randint(0, 10000, n_samples),\n        'dst_bytes': np.random.randint(0, 10000, n_samples),\n        'flag': np.random.choice(flags, n_samples),\n        'land': np.random.binomial(1, 0.05, n_samples),\n        'wrong_fragment': np.random.randint(0, 3, n_samples),\n        'urgent': np.random.randint(0, 2, n_samples),\n    }\n    df = pd.DataFrame(data)\n    malicious_prob = (\n        0.2 * (df['src_bytes'] > 5000).astype(float) +\n        0.2 * (df['wrong_fragment'] > 0).astype(float) +\n        0.2 * (df['urgent'] > 0).astype(float) +\n        0.1 * (df['protocol_type'] == 'icmp').astype(float) +\n        0.1 * (df['flag'] == 'REJ').astype(float)\n    )\n    labels = np.random.binomial(1, malicious_prob.clip(0, 0.95))\n    df['label'] = labels\n    return df\n\nfrom sklearn.preprocessing import StandardScaler, LabelEncoder\n\ndef preprocess_network_data(df):\n    X = df.drop('label', axis=1)\n    y = df['label'].values\n    for col in ['protocol_type', 'service', 'flag']:\n        le = LabelEncoder()\n        X[col] = le.fit_transform(X[col])\n    scaler = StandardScaler()\n    X_scaled = scaler.fit_transform(X)\n    return X_scaled, y\n\ndef build_dnn_model(input_dim):\n    model = models.Sequential([\n        layers.Input(shape=(input_dim,)),\n        layers.Dense(32, activation='relu'),\n        layers.Dense(16, activation='relu'),\n        layers.Dense(1, activation='sigmoid')\n    ])\n    model.compile(\n        optimizer='adam',\n        loss='binary_crossentropy',\n        metrics=['accuracy']\n    )\n    return model\n\ndef prepare_cifar10_animals_vehicles():\n    (X_train, np.isin(y, vehicle_classes)\n        X_animal = X[idx_animal]\n        y_animal = np.zeros(X_animal.shape[0], dtype=int)\n        X_vehicle = X[idx_vehicle]\n        y_vehicle = np.ones(X_vehicle.shape[0], dtype=int)\n        X_filtered = np.concatenate([X_animal, X_vehicle], axis=0)\n        y_filtered = np.concatenate([y_animal, y_vehicle], axis=0)\n        return X_filtered, y_filtered\n\n    X_train_f, y_train_f = filter_data(X_train, y_train)\n    X_test_f, y_test_f = filter_data(X_test, y_test)\n    X_train_f = X_train_f.astype('float32') / 255.0\n    X_test_f = X_test_f.astype('float32') / 255.0\n    idx = np.arange(X_train_f.shape[0])\n    np.random.shuffle(idx)\n    X_train_f, y_train_f = X_train_f[idx], y_train_f[idx]\n    idx = np.arange(X_test_f.shape[0])\n    np.random.shuffle(idx)\n    X_test_f, y_test_f = X_test_f[idx], y_test_f[idx]\n    return X_train_f, X_test_f, y_train_f, y_test_f\n\ndef build_transfer_cnn(input_shape):\n    base_model = applications.MobileNetV2(\n        input_shape=input_shape, include_top=False, weights=None, pooling='avg'\n    )\n    base_model.trainable = False\n Features: duration, protocol_type, service, src_bytes, dst_bytes, flag, land, wrong_fragment, urgent\n    Label: 0 (safe), 1 (malicious)\n    \"\"\"\n    protocols = ['tcp', 'udp', 'icmp']\n    services = ['http', 'ftp', 'smtp', 'dns', 'ssh']\n    flags = ['SF', 'S0', 'REJ', 'RSTR']\n    \n    data = {\n        'duration': np.random.exponential(scale=2, size=n_samples),\n        'protocol_type': np.random.choice(protocols, n_samples),\n        'service': np.random.choice(services, n_samples),\n        'src_bytes': np.random.randint(0, 10000, n_samples),\n        'dst_bytes': np.random.randint(0, 10000, n_samples),\n        'flag': np.random.choice(flags, n_samples),\n        'land': np.random.binomial(1, 0.05, n_samples),\n        'wrong_fragment': np.random.randint(0, 3, n_samples),\n        'urgent': np.random.randint(0, 2, n_samples),\n    }\n    df = pd.DataFrame(data)\n    \n    # Simple logic: traffic with high src_bytes, wrong_fragment, or urgent is more likely malicious\n    malicious_prob = (\n        0.2 * (df['src_bytes'] > 5000).astype(float) +\n        0.2 * (df['wrong_fragment'] > 0).astype(float) +\n        0.2 * (df['urgent'] > 0).astype(float) +\n        0.1 * (df['protocol_type'] == 'icmp').astype(float) +\n        0.1 * (df['flag'] == 'REJ').astype(float)\n    )\n    labels = np.random.binomial(1, malicious_prob.clip(0, 0.95))\n    df['label'] classification.\n    \"\"\"\n    model = models.Sequential([\n        layers.Input(shape=(input_dim,)),\n        layers.Dense(32, activation='relu'),\n        layers.Dense(16, activation='relu'),\n        layers.Dense(1, activation='sigmoid')\n    ])\n    model.compile(\n        optimizer='adam',\n        loss='binary_crossentropy',\n        metrics=['accuracy']\n    )\n    return model\n\ndef CNN for Image Classification (Animals vs Vehicles)\n#####################################\n\ndef prepare_cifar10_animals_vehicles():\n    \"\"\"\n    Load CIFAR-10 and select animals (cat, dog, horse, deer, frog, bird) and vehicles (automobile, truck, airplane, ship).\n    Returns X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test where y=0 for animal, y=1 for vehicle.\n    \"\"\"\n    print(\"\\n=== CNN: Image Classification (Animals vs Vehicles) ===\")\n    (X_train, y_train), (X_test, y_test) = tf.keras.datasets.cifar10.load_data()\n    y_train = y_train.flatten()\n    y_test = y_test.flatten()\n    # CIFAR-10 classes\n    animal_classes = [2, 3, 4, 5, 6, 7]  # bird, cat, deer, dog, frog, horse\n    vehicle_classes = [0, 1, 8, 9]        # airplane, automobile, ship, truck\n    \n    def filter_data(X, y):\n        idx_animal = np.isin(y, animal_classes)\n        idx_vehicle = np.isin(y, vehicle_classes)\n        X_animal = X[idx_animal]\n        y_animal = np.zeros(X_animal.shape[0], dtype=int)\n        X_vehicle = X[idx_vehicle]\n        y_vehicle = np.ones(X_vehicle.shape[0], dtype=int)\n        X_filtered = np.concatenate([X_animal, X_vehicle], axis=0)\n        y_filtered = np.concatenate([y_animal, y_vehicle], axis=0)\n        return X_filtered, y_filtered\n    \n    X_train_f, y_train_f = filter_data(X_train, y_train)\n    X_test_f, y_test_f = filter_data(X_test, y_test)\n    \n    # Normalize images\n    X_train_f = X_train_f.astype('float32') / 255.0\n    X_test_f = X_test_f.astype('float32') / 255.0\n    \n    # Shuffle\n    idx = np.arange(X_train_f.shape[0])\n    np.random.shuffle(idx)\n    X_train_f, y_train_f = X_train_f[idx], y_train_f[idx]\n    \n    idx = np.arange(X_test_f.shape[0])\n    np.random.shuffle(idx)\n    X_test_f, y_test_f = X_test_f[idx], y_test_f[idx]\n    \n    return X_train_f, X_test_f, y_train_f, y_test_f\n\ndef build_transfer_cnn(input_shape):\n    \"\"\"\n    Build a CNN using transfer learning from MobileNetV2.\n    \"\"\"\n    base_model = applications.MobileNetV2(\n        input_shape=input_shape, include_top=False, weights='imagenet', pooling='avg'\n    )\n    base_model.trainable = False  # Freeze base\n    model = models.Sequential([\n        base_model,\n        layers.Dense(128, activation='relu'),\n        layers.Dropout(0.3),\n        layers.Dense(1, activation='sigmoid')\n    ])\n    model.compile(\n        optimizer='adam',\n        loss='binary_crossentropy',\n        metrics=['accuracy']\n    )\n    return model\n\ndef evaluate_cnn_classification(y_true, y_pred, y_prob):\n    \"\"\"\n    Print evaluation metrics for CNN binary classification.\n    \"\"\"\n    print(\"Accuracy:  {:.4f}\".format(accuracy_score(y_true, y_pred)))\n    print(\"Precision: {:.4f}\".format(precision_score(y_true, y_pred)))\n    print(\"Recall:    {:.4f}\".format(recall_score(y_true, y_pred)))\n    print(\"F1 Score:  {:.4f}\".format(f1_score(y_true, y_pred)))\n    print(\"\\nClassification Report:\\n\", classification_report(y_true, y_pred, target_names=['Animal','Vehicle']))\n    cm = confusion_matrix(y_true, y_pred)\n    plt.figure(figsize=(4, 4))\n    plt.imshow(cm, cmap='Blues')\n    plt.title(\"Confusion Matrix\")\n    plt.xlabel(\"Predicted\")\n    plt.ylabel(\"Actual\")\n    plt.colorbar()\n    plt.xticks([0,1], ['Animal','Vehicle'])\n    plt.yticks([0,1], ['Animal','Vehicle'])\n    for i in range(2):\n        for j in range(2):\n            plt.text(j, i, cm[i, j], ha='center', va='center', color='red')\n    plt.tight_layout()\n    plt.show()\n\ndef cnn_image_classification_pipeline():\n    \"\"\"\n    Pipeline for CNN-based image classification (animals vs vehicles) using transfer learning.\n    \"\"\"\n    X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = prepare_cifar10_animals_vehicles()\n    # Check probabilities in [0,1]\n        self.assertTrue(np.all((result[\"y_prob\"] >= 0) & (result[\"y_prob\"] <= 1)))\n\n    def test_dnn_network_traffic_pipeline_edge_cases(self):\n        # All safe\n        df = generate_synthetic_network_data(n_samples=10)\n        df['label'] = 0\n        X, y = preprocess_network_data(df)\n        model = build_dnn_model(X.shape[1])\n        # Should not crash on all one class\n        model.fit(X, y, epochs=1, batch_size=2, verbose=0)\n        y_prob = model.predict(X).flatten()\n        y_pred = (y_prob > 0.5).astype(int)\n        self.assertTrue(np.all(y_pred == 0))\n        # All malicious\n        df['label'] = 1\n        X, y = preprocess_network_data(df)\n        model = build_dnn_model(X.shape[1])\n        model.fit(X, y, epochs=1, batch_size=2, verbose=0)\n        y_prob = model.predict(X).flatten()\n        y_pred = (y_prob > 0.5).astype(int)\n        self.assertTrue(np.all(y_pred == 1))\n\n
